2025-02-10 09:23:26 UTC prinsz.dom: class MyHeart:  
    def __init__(self):  
        # My heart has infinite energy when I'm with you  
        self.energy = float('inf')  
        # My heart is always running at max speed when I see you  
        self.state = "Overclocked"  
        # The one who makes my system work perfectly—you <3  
        self.target = "You"  

    def on_see_you(self):  
        print("Heart rate increasing...")  # My heartbeat gets faster  
        print("Brain processing at max efficiency...")  # My thoughts focus only on you  
        print("Gravity towards you: Unbreakable")  # I can't resist being near you  

    def love_forever(self):  
        # This loop runs forever—just like my love for you  
        while True:  
            print("I love you <3")  

# Creating "me" as an object of MyHeart  
me = MyHeart()  
me.on_see_you()  # Simulates what happens when I see you  
me.love_forever()  # My love for you never stops
